```r
PA_latlong <- left_join(PA, latlong, by = "county") %>%
  arrange(desc(value))
head(PA_latlong)
```

mapping

```r
PAmap <- leaflet() %>%
  addTiles() %>%
  addCircleMarkers(data = q4,
                   color = "green",
                   popup = ~county,
                   label = ~countyname.x) %>%
  addCircleMarkers(data = q3,
                   color = "yellow",
                   popup = ~county,
                   label = ~countyname.x) %>%
  addCircleMarkers(data = q2,
                   color = "blue",
                   popup = ~county,
                   label = ~countyname.x) %>%
  addCircleMarkers(data = q1,
                   color = "red",
                   popup = ~county,
                   label = ~countyname.x) %>%
  addCircleMarkers(data = topPAcounty,
                   color = "pink",
                   popup = ~county,
                   label = ~countyname.x)
```
